Univers Light Regular (Univers-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Univers-Light', Everything looks good.

Please verify against job spec.
MS NID 13 is:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype here: www.monotype.com
but should be:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

Univers Light Regular (Univers-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Univers' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Univers Light'.

Univers Condensed Regular (universc.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Univers-Condensed', Everything looks good.

Pass

Univers Condensed Regular (universc.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
'space' in NID 6 cause issues in fontbook for Mac.

NID 6 is 'Univers-Condensed', Everything looks good.

Pass

Univers Condensed Regular (universc.ttf)

name

MS NID 13, License Text

'License Text' has leading or trailing spaces.

leading or trailing spaces are highlighted with [  ]:
'This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software.[  ]You can learn more about Monotype here:[  ]www.monotype.com'

Error

Univers Condensed Regular (universc.ttf)

name

MS NID 8/13

License text if Manufactur (NID 8) is one of these 'Monotype Imaging Inc.', 'Monotype Imaging Inc', 'Monotype ITC Inc.', 'Monotype Hong Kong Limited', 'Monotype Limited', 'Monotype KK', 'Monotype Solutions India Private Limited'

Please verify against job spec.
MS NID 13 is:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype here: www.monotype.com
but should be:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

Pass

Univers Condensed Regular (universc.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

If Typographic Family Name (NID 16) is present Typographic Subfamily Name (NID 17) must contain a value (Windows Preferred).

OK: Font has both Typographic Family Name (NID 16) and Typographic Subfamily Name (NID 17).

Pass

Univers Condensed Regular (universc.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Univers' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Condensed' = NID 1 'Univers Condensed'.

Pass

Univers Condensed Bold (universbc.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.

NID 6 is 'Univers-BoldCondensed', Everything looks good.

Univers Condensed Bold (universbc.ttf)

name

MS NID 8/13

License text if Manufactur (NID 8) is one of these 'Monotype Imaging Inc.', 'Monotype Imaging Inc', 'Monotype ITC Inc.', 'Monotype Hong Kong Limited', 'Monotype Limited', 'Monotype KK', 'Monotype Solutions India Private Limited'

Please verify against job spec.
MS NID 13 is:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype here: www.monotype.com
but should be:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

Critical

Univers Condensed Bold (universbc.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

(NID 16 + 'Space' + NID 17) 'Univers Bold Condensed' ≠ 'Univers Condensed Bold' (NID 1 + 'Space' + NID 2).

Unified Monotype Width Name Rules

Univers Bold (universb.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.

NID 6 is 'Univers-Bold', Everything looks good.

This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement.
